#Made by Lord Bogdanoff
focus_tree = {
	id = belorussia_focus
	country = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 10
			tag = BLR
		}
	}

	# Sets Camera to Opening of the Political Tree
	initial_show_position = { x = 78 y = 1 }
	#Economic branch
	focus = {
		id = BLR_Economic
		icon = coins

		x = 120
		y = 0

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }

		cost = 5

		ai_will_do = { factor = 155 }

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BLR_Economic"
			increase_economic_growth = yes
			calculate_interest_rate = yes
		}
	}
	#European Companies
	focus = {
		id = BLR_European_Companies
		icon = industry_democratic3

		x = 15
		y = 2

		cost = 5

		relative_position_id = BLR_Economic

		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Zianon Pazniak"
					ruling_only = yes
				  }
			}
		}

		prerequisite = { focus = BLR_Economic }

		mutually_exclusive = { focus = BLR_Russia_economic }

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 155
			modifier = {
				factor = 15
				has_global_flag = BLR_DEMOCRATIC_PATH
			}
		}

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BLR_European_Companies"
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 7 }
			change_domestic_influence_percentage = yes
			add_political_power = -50
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
	}

			}

				factor = 50
				has_global_flag = BLR_NATIONALIST_PATH
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 50
				has_global_flag = BLR_COMMUNISM_PATH
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				has_global_flag = BLR_ARMY_PRIORITY
			}
		}

		available = {
		OR = {
			 has_government = communism
			 has_government = nationalist
		}
		}

		mutually_exclusive = { focus = BLR_prof_army }
		mutually_exclusive = { focus = BLR_kvo_army }

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_MILITARY_LAWS }

		prerequisite = { focus = BLR_defence_strategy }

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BLR_army1"
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 22 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.01 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = -0.002 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BLR_outdated_army
				add_idea = BLR_reforming_army
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = no_military }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = no_military
					add_idea = partial_draft_army
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = volunteer_army }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = volunteer_army
					add_idea = partial_draft_army
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = draft_army }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = draft_army
					add_idea = partial_draft_army
				}
			}
			block_conscription_change = yes
		}
	}

				picture = "tacciana_holubiewa.dds"

				traits = {
					emerging_Communist-State
				}
